type\")\n\t}\n\n\treturn matches, msg, nil\n}\n\nconst (\n\tpercentMultiplier = 10000\n)\n\nfunc matchesString(c storage.EvaluationConstraint, v string) bool {\n\tswitch c.Operator {\n\tcase
